    },
    "content": {
      "rendered": "<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">When thinking about this year&#8217;s Coach of the Year we kept going back and forth on who it should be. Multiple people Deserved the Honor, but when we started to narrow it down,  two names kept coming up. We justified both being named the sole coach of the year, But the more we talked, and the more we thought about it, it became clear, we could not give it to just one of them. So we settled on Co-Coaches of the Year. Kyle Surprenant of John A. Logan and Jeff Willis of LSU-Eunice take home the Honors this year.</span></p>\n<p>&nbsp;</p>\n<h1 style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Kyle Surprenant- John A. Logan</span></h1>\n<p><img data-attachment-id=\"11173\" data-permalink=\"https://thejbb.net/2020/04/24/2020-coaches-of-the-year/kyle-surprenat-2-coty/\" data-orig-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/thejbb.net/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/Kyle-Surprenat-2-COTY.jpg?fit=525%2C377&amp;ssl=1\" data-orig-size=\"525,377\" data-comments-opened=\"1\" data-image-meta=\"{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}\" data-image-title=\"Kyle Surprenat 2 COTY\" data-image-description=\"\" data-medium-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/thejbb.net/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/Kyle-Surprenat-2-COTY.jpg?fit=300%2C215&amp;ssl=1\" data-large-file=\"https://i1.wp.com/thejbb.net/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/Kyle-Surprenat-2-COTY.jpg?fit=525%2C377&amp;ssl=1\" class=\"size-medium wp-image-11173 aligncenter\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/thejbb.net/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/Kyle-Surprenat-2-COTY.jpg?resize=300%2C215&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"\" width=\"300\" height=\"215\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/thejbb.net/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/Kyle-Surprenat-2-COTY.jpg?resize=300%2C215&amp;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/thejbb.net/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/Kyle-Surprenat-2-COTY.jpg?w=525&amp;ssl=1 525w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">I mean what else is there to say… 20-1 record, remained in the top three for the entire season and  at one point they were on a 18 game win streak. Surprenant led the Vols to a final #1 spot and the Vols are well prepped for the future as well. The Vols are one of the best teams top to bottom this year. They were loaded with depth where you did not need depth, With Countless guys (14 Plus) receiving offers to play at the next level, and a full squad  of guys buying into the culture that started at the top. Surprenant Had high hopes for this season and for good reason. We here at the JBB believe that Surprenant had built a team that had what it would take to bring home the Title at the end of the season if the season would have gotten a chance to play itself out. </span></p>\n<p>&nbsp;</p>\n<h1 style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Jeff Willis- LSU-Eunice</span></h1>\n<p><img data-attachment-id=\"11172\" data-permalink=\"https://thejbb.net/2020/04/24/2020-coaches-of-the-year/jeff-willis-coty/\" data-orig-file=\"https://i2.wp.com/thejbb.net/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/Jeff-Willis-COTY.jpg?fit=525%2C377&amp;ssl=1\" data-orig-size=\"525,377\" data-comments-opened=\"1\" data-image-meta=\"{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}\" data-image-title=\"Jeff Willis COTY\" data-image-description=\"\" data-medium-file=\"https://i2.wp.com/thejbb.net/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/Jeff-Willis-COTY.jpg?fit=300%2C215&amp;ssl=1\" data-large-file=\"https://i2.wp.com/thejbb.net/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/Jeff-Willis-COTY.jpg?fit=525%2C377&amp;ssl=1\" class=\"alignnone size-medium wp-image-11172 aligncenter\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/thejbb.net/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/Jeff-Willis-COTY.jpg?resize=300%2C215&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"\" width=\"300\" height=\"215\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/thejbb.net/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/Jeff-Willis-COTY.jpg?resize=300%2C215&amp;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/thejbb.net/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/Jeff-Willis-COTY.jpg?w=525&amp;ssl=1 525w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Anytime you can have an undefeated team that says something. Anytime you can do it in the fashion that Eunice did it is even more Special. When you look back at what could have happened this year you are just left to wonder whether this was going to be one of the all-time great teams in Juco history. Jeff has been a staple at LSU-Eunice for years; Bringing home National Titles, Multiple All-Americans, and many other honors. But when you look at this year&#8217;s team and look at how they were winning you could tell that this team had bought into Jeffs Culture and how he wanted things to run. Winning games by an average of just over 10 runs a game. This year was going to be special for the Bengals. </span></p>\n",

font-variant: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">. </span><a style=\"text-decoration: none;\" href=\"https://thejbb.net/?s=orange+coast+\"><span style=\"font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: #ffffff; background-color: transparent; font-weight: 400; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; text-decoration: underline; -webkit-text-decoration-skip: none; text-decoration-skip-ink: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">Santa Ana</span></a><span style=\"font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: #ffffff; background-color: transparent; font-weight: 400; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\"> was another Orange Empire Conference team that was gearing up to jump into that gauntlet. </span></p><p><b style=\"font-weight: normal;\"> </b></p><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt;\"><a style=\"text-decoration: none;\" href=\"https://thejbb.net/?s=santa+rosa\"><span style=\"font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: #ffffff; background-color: transparent; font-family: Arial; color: #ffffff; background-color: transparent; font-weight: 400; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\"> started the season ranked 13th and moved up every week finishing at #5. They finished with a 18-2 record with key wins over Feather River, a Series win over Sac City it was clear to see they were on the rise. They really had no sign of letting up. They would have finished the season with back to back series between them Modesto and San Joaquin Delta to most likely decide the winner of the Big 8 Conference.</span></p><p><b style=\"font-weight: normal;\"> </b></p><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: #ffffff; background-color: transparent; font-weight: 400; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">Sacramento City spent the majority of the season ranked #2 before falling to #6 in week 7. They remained there in the final ranking. They finished the season with a 16-4 record. To start the season they rallied off 9 wins before losing their first game to </span><a style=\"text-decoration: none;\" href=\"https://thejbb.net/?s=Fresno+city\"><span style=\"font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: #ffffff; background-color: transparent; font-weight: 400; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; text-decoration: underline; -webkit-text-decoration-skip: none; text-decoration-skip-ink: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">Fresno City</span></a><span style=\"font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: #ffffff; background-color: transparent; font-weight: 400; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">. The only blemish that they have had was their series loss to </span><a style=\"text-decoration: none;\" href=\"https://thejbb.net/?s=santa+rosa\"><span style=\"font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: #ffffff; background-color: transparent; font-weight: 400; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; text-decoration: underline; -webkit-text-decoration-skip: none; text-decoration-skip-ink: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">Santa Rosa</span></a><span style=\"font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: #ffffff; background-color: transparent; font-weight: 400; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">. </span></p><p><b style=\"font-weight: normal;\"> </b></p><p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height: 1.38; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt;\"><a style=\"text-decoration: none;\" href=\"https://thejbb.net/?s=saddleback\"><span style=\"font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: #ffffff; background-color: transparent; font-weight: 400; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; text-decoration: underline; -webkit-text-decoration-skip: none; text-decoration-skip-ink: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\">Saddleback</span></a><span style=\"font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: #ffffff; background-color: transparent; font-weight: 400; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;\"> sat in the Teens for most of the season before jumping into the top 10 in week 7. They remain in that spot to end the season. With a 16-4 record, they had big series wins over </span><a style=\"text-decoration: none;\" href=\"https://thejbb.net/?s=santa+barbara\"><span style=\"font-size: 11pt; font-family: Arial; color: #ffffff;       "rendered": "<p>Teams of The Week</p>\n<p>Here is a look at the teams that made the biggest moves or had huge weeks as a team for each division</p>\n<p>Div 1: Kansas City Kansas (4-1)</p>\n<p>As stated in this week's new Next 5 Out, KCK made a huge jump this past week. They went 4-1 on the week, winning their weekend series against the then ranked #6 3 games to 1. </p>\n<p>KCK started their week with a mid-week game against state fair in which they won 19-1. After falling behind 1-0 in the bottom of the first KCK tied it up in the second then scored in the 5th, 7th, 8th, and then scored 9 in the 9th. Leading them in that game was Tre Simmons who got the Start and the wing going 7 innings striking out 3 while giving up the lone run. At the plate 3 Blue Devils had homers, Griffin Everitt (1-4, 2 RBI), Jose Sosa (4-6, 5 RBI, Double) and Trey Hoover (1-4, 2 RBI). </p>\n<p>To start their weekend they took the first 3 games against Cowley before dropping the final game of the weekend. </p>\n<p>The first two games they took at home 6-5 and 14-8. They then took the first game at Cowley 9-8 before dropping the final game 18-1. </p>\n<p>Div 2: Northeast Mississippi (6-0)</p>\n<p>Northeast has been one of the Fastest rising Division 2 teams this season. Starting in the 50’s and now find themselves sitting at #7 in the country. This past week they played 6 games between Wednesday and Sunday winning all of them. </p>\n<p>They started Wednesday with a doubleheader win against Jackson State taking game 1 6-4 and game 2 8-0. </p>\n<p>Heading into the weekend they had a 4-game series against Marshalltown. They took game 1 2-1 behind a strong pitching performance by Dylan Hitchcock who went 5.2 Innings striking out 10. In-game 2, the won 13-3 in just 5 innings due to a run rule. Conner Davis and Jacob Compton both helped put up the runs. Davis was 1-4 with a double and 2 RBI’s while also scoring 3 runs. Compton was 1-3 with 3 RBI’s. </p>\n<p>In their Sunday Double Header, It started how the Saturday games ended. By Run Rule. In just 5 innings they won 14-1. The game was led by the bat of Hayes Hansford who was 4-4 in the game with a double, homer, 5 RBI’s and a run. Sunday's second game was a bit closer in a 7-4 win. Compton showed up again going 3-4 in the game with 2 doubles, a Home Runs and 4 RBI’s. </p>\n<div class=\"pmpro_content_message\">This content is for 1-Year, 2-Year, 5-Year, 5-Year (Paid-in-Full), and 2-Year (Paid-in-Full) members only.<br /><a href=\"http://thejbb.net/wp-login.php\">Log In</a> <a href=\"http://thejbb.net/wp-login.php?action=register\">Register</a></div>",

elementor-clearfix\"><p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Another week with more unfolding. More teams are starting, tons of games happening all over the place, and even more movement!</span></p><p style=\"text-align: center;\"> </p><h1 style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><u>NJCAA Division 1</u></span></h1><p style=\"text-align: center;\"> </p><p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The top 5 stayed the same this week:</span></p><p style=\"text-align: center;\"> </p><ul style=\"text-align: center;\"><li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">John A. Logan was 3-1 on the week dropping their first game of the season to Lincoln Land</span></li><li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Wabash Valley went 4-0 this past week putting up 57 runs across those 4 games</span></li><li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Yavapai lost an early week game to Arizona Western but finished the week 3-1 pushing them to 22-3 on the season. They are still someone not alone at the top of the ACCAC. They are currently tied with South Mountain at 12-2 in conference. </span></li><li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">McLennan dropped one game this past week to North Central Texas in their Saturday double header but finished the week 4-1. </span></li><li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Iowa Western rounds out the top 5 after a 4-0 week. </span></li></ul><p style=\"text-align: center;\"> </p><p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">This is where things at the Division 1 level start to change. </span></p><ul style=\"text-align: center;\"><li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Crowder continues their winning ways and brings their record to 20-1, with the only loss coming to currently ranked #5 Iowa Western back on February 22nd. They had a 7-0 week which jumps them up 3 spots to #6. </span></li></ul><ul style=\"text-align: center;\"><li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Johnson County jumps up 3 spots to #7. They were 4-0. They swept Labetta in a 4 game series in which they outscored them 67-7. With a 32-0 game in the final game of the series. </span></li><li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Grayson stays at #8 after a 3-1 week. They started with a win against San Jac on monday and then took 2 of the 3 against Murray state over the weekend. </span></li><li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Northwest Florida moves into the to 10 for the first time this season coming in at #9 this week. They were 4-1 this past week with the only loss coming from splitting a double header with Div 2 power Pearl Rivers.</span></li><li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">San Jac rounds out the top 10. They were 3-1 on the week dropping an early week game to Grayson. </span></li></ul><p style=\"text-align: center;\"> </p><p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Another Notable Moves:</span></p><ul style=\"text-align: center;\"><li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Eastern Oklahoma State Jumps 11 Spots to #11</span></li><li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Walter State Jumps 7 to #12</span></li><li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Odessa Jumps 7 to #14</span></li><li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Snead State goes from Unranked to #24</span></li></ul><p style=\"text-align: center;\"> </p><h1 style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><u>NJCAA Division 2</u></span></h1><p style=\"text-align: center;\"> </p><p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Like the Division 1 level the division 2 level top 3 remained the same but there was some shuffling.</span></p><ul style=\"text-align: center;\"><li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">LSU-Eunice remains at #1 pushing their season record to 20-0. </span></li><li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Pearl River jumps up 1 spot to #2 after going 4-1 on the week with the only loss coming form Division 1 power Northwest Florida</span></li><li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">NOC-Tonkawa drop 1 spot to #3. They were 6-2 on the week splitting with new region 2 opponent North Central Missouri.</span></li></ul><p style=\"text-align: center;\"> </p><p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">This is where a lot of movement starts to happen at this level.</span></p><ul style=\"text-align: center;\"><li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Sinclair jumps up 2 spots to #4 after a 5-0 week.</span></li><li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Mesa drops 1 spot to #5 after splitting with both Chandler-Gilbert and Paradise Valley</span></li><li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Northwest Mississippi move up 2 to #6 going 4-0 pushing them to 14-1 on the season</span></li><li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Northeast Mississippi move up 2 to #7 going 6-0 pushing them to 16-2 on the season</span></li><li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Hinds rounds out a third straight Mississippi team at #8 going 1-1 on the week splitting with baton Rouge which brings them to 11-1 on the season</span></li><li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Kankakee drop 4 to #9 after going 1-1 on the week dropping a game to Parkland.</span></li><li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Southeastern dropped 3 to #10 after going 2-2 on the week splitting with Itawamba and Mississippi Delta. </span></li></ul><p style=\"text-align: center;\"> </p><p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Other Notable Moves:</span></p><ul style=\"text-align: center;\"><li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Parkland jump 3 to #12</span></li><li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Patrick Henry go from Unranked to #21</span></li><li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span Unranked to #25</span></li></ul><p style=\"text-align: center;\"> </p><h1 style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><u>NJCAA Division 3</u></span></h1><p style=\"text-align: center;\"> </p><p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">With a lot of teams just starting at this level things are about to start shaping up. </span></p><ul style=\"text-align: center;\"><li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Rowan Gloucester dropped one game to Mercer County but still remain on top with a 3-1
